        function serialize(obj) {

            .map(function(key) {
              return [key, obj[key]].join('=');
            })
            .join('&');
        }

        function getCookie(name) {
          var matches = d.cookie.match(new RegExp('(?:^|; )' + name.replace(/([\.$?*|{}\(\)\[\]\\\/\+^])/g, '\\$1') + '=([^;]*)'));

        }
